%------------------------------
\begin{letter}{a}
\newentry
\homograph{1}%
\headword{a}%
\hypertarget{hvo11537}{}%
\ipa{à}%
%
%
\synpos{art}%
\hypertarget{hvo40149}{}%
\definition{the}%
\lsgloss{the}%
{\startexample}%
\hypertarget{hvo10231}{}%
\vernacular{à bʊ̃́ʊ̃́ná tʃɪ́ɛ́ŋɪ̃̀ à vìí bárá bálɪ̀ɛ̀.}%
\hypertarget{hvo10231}{}%
\modvernacular{à bʊ̃́ʊ̃́\-ná tʃɪ́ɛ́\-ŋɪ̃̀ à vìí bá\-rá bá\-lɪ̀ɛ̀.}%
\hypertarget{hvo26811}{}%
\trs{The goats have broken the cooking pots in two parts.}%
%------------------------------
\newentry
\homograph{2}%
\headword{a}%
\hypertarget{hvo20824}{}%
\ipa{à}%
%
%
\synpos{conn}%
\hypertarget{hvo36660}{}%
\definition{and, then}%
\lsgloss{and; then}%
{\startexample}
\exnr{1}%
\hypertarget{hvo3056}{}%
\vernacular{ʊ̀ fɪ̀ɪ̀ wíò à tʃá tàmá ká ʊ́ sʊ́wà, nɪ́ŋ wā ʊ̀ kpégéó.}%
\hypertarget{hvo3056}{}%
\modvernacular{ʊ̀ fɪ̀ɪ̀ wíò à tʃá tà\-má ká ʊ́ sʊ́\-wà, nɪ́ŋ wā ʊ̀ kpé\-géó.}%
\hypertarget{hvo7420}{}%
\trs{He was very ill and almost died, but now he is well.}%
\exnr{2}%
\hypertarget{hvo44110}{}%
\vernacular{ùù bìé tʃʊ́ŋá à kpáámá à lɪ̀ɪ̀ kùó dɪ̀ wāā à tʃèlè, ámúŋ̀ tʃɔ̀rɪ̀gɪ̀.}%
\hypertarget{hvo44110}{}%
\modvernacular{ùù bìé tʃʊ́\-ŋá à kpáá\-má à lɪ̀ɪ̀ kùó dɪ̀ wāā à tʃè\-lè, á\-múŋ̀ tʃɔ̀rɪ̀gɪ̀.}%
\hypertarget{hvo28891}{}%
\trs{His child carried the yams from farm and fell on his way back, they were all smashed.}%
%------------------------------
\newentry
\homograph{3}%
\headword{a}%
\hypertarget{hvo36792}{}%
\ipa{à}%
%\varblockopener{}%
\typefocvar{\hyperlink{hvo30778}{aa}}%
%\varblockcloser{}%
%
\synpos{pro}%
\hypertarget{hvo13968}{}%
\definition{non-human third person plural pronoun}%
\lsgloss{they (hum-)}%
{\startexample}
\exnr{1}%
\hypertarget{hvo36483}{}%
\vernacular{vááwísē há wà lɪ́ɪ̀, à há wà lálɪ̀ síé.}%
\hypertarget{hvo36483}{}%
\modvernacular{váá\-wísē há wà lɪ́ɪ̀, à há wà lá\-lɪ̀ síé.}%
\hypertarget{hvo7947}{}%
\trs{The puppies are not going out since they have not yet opened their eyes.}%
\exnr{2}%
\hypertarget{hvo30493}{}%
\vernacular{bà kàá dɪ̀ búúrè á sííū.}%
\hypertarget{hvo30493}{}%
\modvernacular{bà kàá dɪ̀ búú\-rè á sííū.}%
\hypertarget{hvo43237}{}%
\trs{They will want them to grow bigger.}%

\newentry
\hypertarget{hvo18936}{}%
\headword{amɪ̃ɛ̃}%
\hypertarget{hvo26537}{}%
\ipa{àmɪ̃̀ɛ̃̀}%
%
%
\synpos{conn}%
\hypertarget{hvo13750}{}%
\definition{particle confirming a proposition that was stated or is contextually inferred as premise e.g. if so, in that case}%
\lsgloss{if so; in that case}%
{\startexample}
\exnr{1}%
\hypertarget{hvo44684}{}%
\vernacular{àmɪ̃̀ɛ̃̀ dɪ̀ nàmɪ̃̀ã́ wáá tùò à sɪ̀ɪ̀máá nɪ̄ ɪ̀ wàá dȉȉ?}%
\hypertarget{hvo44684}{}%
\modvernacular{à\-mɪ̃̀ɛ̃̀ dɪ̀ nà\-mɪ̃̀ã́ wáá tùò à sɪ̀ɪ̀máá nɪ̄ ɪ̀ wàá dȉȉ?}%
\hypertarget{hvo37430}{}%
\trs{So, if there is no meat in the food you won't eat?}%
\exnr{2}%
\hypertarget{hvo42114}{}%
\vernacular{dɪ̀ bákúríí dí kʊ̀ʊ̀ dɪ̀à hán nɪ̄ zàāǹ, àmɪ̃̀ɛ̃̀ ǹ wàà tùò nī. }%
\hypertarget{hvo42114}{}%
\modvernacular{dɪ̀ bá\-kúríí dí kʊ̀ʊ̀ dɪ̀à hán nɪ̄ zàāǹ, à\-mɪ̃̀ɛ̃̀ ǹ wàà tùò nī. }%
\hypertarget{hvo24976}{}%
\trs{If Bakuri eats food in this house today, then I am not here (If I were to be here, he would not get a chance).}%

\trs{Who is coming here?}%

\lsgloss{spot}%

\hypertarget{hvo30030}{}%
\trs{These spots on my pants are black.}%
\exnr{2}%
\hypertarget{hvo18384}{}%
\vernacular{tʃìtʃàvɛ̀tɪ́ɪ̀ dʊ́á ɪ̀ nã̀ã̀tɔ́wá báámà nɪ̄.}%
\hypertarget{hvo18384}{}%

\trs{There are spots of mud on your shoes.}%

\newentry
\homograph{1}%
\headword{bire}%
\hypertarget{hvo27056}{}%
\ipa{bĭ́ré}%
\pos{v}%
%
%
\sensenr{1}%
\hypertarget{hvo19733}{}%
\definition{to be dark, to make dark}%
\lsgloss{dark}%
{\startexample}
\exnr{1}%
\hypertarget{hvo29502}{}%
\vernacular{tɪ̀ɛ̀ bár bíré ká jā káálɪ̀ dɪ̀á.}%
\hypertarget{hvo29502}{}%
\modvernacular{tɪ̀ɛ̀ bár bí\-ré ká jā káá\-lɪ̀ dɪ̀á.}%
\hypertarget{hvo4858}{}%
\trs{Let it be dark before we go home.}%
\exnr{2}%
\hypertarget{hvo8636}{}%
\vernacular{ʊ̀ ká wà bɪ́ bíré ʊ̀ ká wà bɪ́ sɪ́árɪ́.}%
\hypertarget{hvo8636}{}%
\modvernacular{ʊ̀ ká wà bɪ́ bí\-ré ʊ̀ ká wà bɪ́ sɪ́á\-rɪ́.}%
\hypertarget{hvo31826}{}%
\trs{It is not yet totally black and not totally red.}%
\sensenr{2}%
\hypertarget{hvo3338}{}%
\definition{to be black, to make black}%
\lsgloss{black (be)}%
{\startexample}%
\hypertarget{hvo41626}{}%
\vernacular{à bìè kpá dóŋó bíré ǹ̩ǹ̩ dɪ̀à múŋ̀.}%
\hypertarget{hvo41626}{}%
\modvernacular{à bìè kpá dó\-ŋó bí\-ré ǹ̩ǹ̩ dɪ̀à múŋ̀.}%
\hypertarget{hvo18357}{}%
\trs{The child used dirt to make my house black.}%
\etymology{}%
\etymologysrc{Gur}%
\etymologygloss{dark}%
\etymologycloser{}%

\hypertarget{hvo18935}{}%
\modvernacular{jà wí\-ré jà kɪ́\-ná rá à\-ká và\-là gó dùù\-sèé múŋ̀ nã̀ã̀vàĺ bɪ́\-tōrò.}%
\hypertarget{hvo25225}{}%
\trs{We undress and walk around the whole Ducie three times.}%
\exnr{2}%
\hypertarget{hvo15647}{}%
\vernacular{ʊ̀ bɪ́ kʊ̀ɔ̀rɛ̀ sã̀ã̀ ʊ̀ dɪ̀à rá.}%
\hypertarget{hvo15647}{}%
\modvernacular{ʊ̀ bɪ́ kʊ̀ɔ̀rɛ̀ sã̀ã̀ ʊ̀ dɪ̀à rá.}%
\hypertarget{hvo18606}{}%
\trs{He rebuilt his house.}%

\trs{Leave your book, you are almost asleep.}%

\newentry
\hypertarget{hvo20176}{}%
\headword{daarɪ}%
\hypertarget{hvo43900}{}%
\ipa{dáárɪ́}%
%
%
\synpos{v}%
\hypertarget{hvo27659}{}%
\definition{to take off the top, as in removing a dried layer of t.z. or porridge, leaves on the surface of the water, or as in shelling membrane from egg, to dig and scratch only the surface}%
\lsgloss{take off the top; dig}%
{\startexample}
\exnr{1}%
\hypertarget{hvo8318}{}%
\vernacular{dáárɪ́ à nɪ́ɪ́ ɲúú kɪ̀ndóŋó tɪ́ŋ tà.}%
\hypertarget{hvo8318}{}%
\modvernacular{dáá\-rɪ́ à nɪ́ɪ́ ɲúú kɪ̀n\-dóŋó tɪ́ŋ tà.}%
\hypertarget{hvo8761}{}%
\trs{Remove the dirt on the surface of the water.}%
\exnr{2}%
\hypertarget{hvo36699}{}%
\vernacular{dáárɪ́ à hàglɪ́búmmò tɪń tà.}%
\hypertarget{hvo36699}{}%
\modvernacular{dáá\-rɪ́ à hàg\-lɪ́\-búmmò tɪń tà.}%
\hypertarget{hvo31873}{}%
\trs{Remove the layer of black soil.}%
\exnr{3}%
\hypertarget{hvo13074}{}%
\vernacular{tɔ́má dáárɪ̀ ʊ̀ dɪ̀ànʊ̃́ã́ rā, ʊ̀ wà bɪ́ gātɪ̄.}%
\hypertarget{hvo13074}{}%
\modvernacular{tɔ́\-má dáá\-rɪ̀ ʊ̀ dɪ̀à\-nʊ̃́ã́ rā, ʊ̀ wà bɪ́ gā\-tɪ̄.}%

\synpos{cpx.v}%

\definition{to entertain, to make things interesting}%

\hypertarget{hvo29419}{}%
\modvernacular{jɪ̀rà hà\-mɔ́\-nà bá wá dáŋ\-ŋɪ́ jà síé.}%
\hypertarget{hvo23853}{}%
\trs{Call the children to come and entertain us.}%

\newentry
\hypertarget{hvo42033}{}%
\headword{degini}%
\hypertarget{hvo23139}{}%
\ipa{dègìnì}%
\pos{v}%
\varblockopener{}%
\typevar{\hyperlink{hvo964}{de\-ŋili}}, \typevar{\hyperlink{hvo9629}{de\-ŋini}}, \typevar{\hyperlink{hvo22979}{de\-geni}}%
\varblockcloser{}%
%
\sensenr{1}%
\hypertarget{hvo14308}{}%
\definition{to put straight, to be straight, to unbend, to set in a direction}%
\lsgloss{straight; set in a direction; unbend}%
{\startexample}
\exnr{1}%
\hypertarget{hvo5189}{}%
\vernacular{tɪ̀ɛ̀ à pítʃɔ́ŋ̀ dègìnì.}%
\hypertarget{hvo5189}{}%
\modvernacular{tɪ̀ɛ̀ à pí\-tʃɔ́ŋ̀ dè\-gìnì.}%
\hypertarget{hvo32525}{}%
\trs{Let the yam mound row be straight.}%
\exnr{2}%
\hypertarget{hvo42565}{}%
\vernacular{tɪ̀ɛ̀ à zɪ̃́ã́ déŋílì.}%
\hypertarget{hvo42565}{}%
\modvernacular{tɪ̀ɛ̀ à zɪ̃́ã́ dé\-ŋílì.}%
\hypertarget{hvo318}{}%
\trs{Let the wall be straight.}%
\sensenr{2}%
\hypertarget{hvo19738}{}%
\definition{tolerant}%
\lsgloss{tolerant}%
{\startexample}%
\hypertarget{hvo23861}{}%
\vernacular{à tɔ́ʊ́tɪ̄ɪ̄nā wā dègìnìjè.}%
\hypertarget{hvo23861}{}%
\modvernacular{à tɔ́ʊ́\-tɪ̄ɪ̄\-nā wā dè\-gìnì\-jè.}%
\hypertarget{hvo12115}{}%
\trs{The landlord is not tolerant.}%
\sensenr{3}%
\hypertarget{hvo13356}{}%
\definition{to be honest, faithful}%
\lsgloss{honest (be); faithful (be)}%
{\startexample}%
\hypertarget{hvo34697}{}%
\vernacular{à bìè dégíníjóó ʊ̀ kà kpá m̩̀m̩̀ mòlèbíí à wà tɪ́ɛ́ŋ.}%
\hypertarget{hvo34697}{}%
\modvernacular{à bìè dé\-gíní\-jóó ʊ̀ kà kpá m̩̀m̩̀ mò\-lèbíí à wà tɪ́ɛ́ŋ.}%
\hypertarget{hvo4865}{}%

\newentry
\hypertarget{hvo1133}{}%
\headword{dɔsɪ}%
\hypertarget{hvo15792}{}%
\ipa{dɔ́sɪ́}%
%
%
\synpos{v}%
\hypertarget{hvo1267}{}%
\definition{to stalk, walk stealthily towards}%
\lsgloss{walk stealthily}%
{\startexample}
\exnr{1}%
\hypertarget{hvo4892}{}%
\vernacular{dɔ́sɪ́ kà kpàgà bʊ̃́ʊ̃́ŋ háŋ̀ tɪ̄ɛ̄ŋ.}%
\hypertarget{hvo4892}{}%
\modvernacular{dɔ́\-sɪ́ kà kpà\-gà bʊ̃́ʊ̃́ŋ háŋ̀ tɪ̄ɛ̄ŋ.}%
\hypertarget{hvo25191}{}%
\trs{Walk stealthily and catch this goat for me.}%
\exnr{2}%

\hypertarget{hvo25931}{}%

\hypertarget{hvo16719}{}%

\hypertarget{hvo37403}{}%
\trs{If you continue over-pruning your cow peas, you will kill them.}%

\hypertarget{hvo6361}{}%
\definition{to lie, to tell untruth}%
\lsgloss{lie}%
{\startexample}%

\hypertarget{hvo21655}{}%
\modvernacular{à bìè hɛ́ŋ\-sɪ́ wɪ́ɛ́ dʊ́ ǹ̩ǹ̩ nʊ̃̀ã̀ nɪ̄ rà.}%
\hypertarget{hvo40795}{}%
\trs{The child lied to me.}%

\lsgloss{rebuke}%

\ipa{jélé}%
%
%
\synpos{v}%

\lsgloss{crow}%

\hypertarget{hvo36709}{}%
\modvernacular{à zím\-báál jé\-lèū.}%
\hypertarget{hvo43978}{}%
\trs{The cock crowed.}%

\vernacular{dʒébúní ànɪ́ ʊ̀ʊ̀ háàŋ jáà júòū.}%
\hypertarget{hvo9782}{}%
\modvernacular{dʒé\-búní à\-nɪ́ ʊ̀ʊ̀ háàŋ jáà júòū.}%
\hypertarget{hvo36250}{}%
\trs{Jebuni and his wife are always fighting.}%

\lsgloss{roof}%

\newentry

\headword{keŋ}%
\hypertarget{hvo7490}{}%
\ipa{keŋ}%
\varblockopener{}%
\typevar{\hyperlink{hvo43854}{ken}}%
\varblockcloser{}%
%
\synpos{adv}%
\hypertarget{hvo28915}{}%
\definition{like that, that, so}%
\lsgloss{like that; that}%
{\startexample}
\exnr{1}%
\hypertarget{hvo29034}{}%
\vernacular{záàŋ ʊ̀ʊ̀ tàá káá zéné kéŋ̀.}%
\hypertarget{hvo29034}{}%
\modvernacular{záàŋ ʊ̀ʊ̀ tàá káá zé\-né kéŋ̀.}%
\hypertarget{hvo21597}{}%
\trs{Today he is talking loudly like that.}%
\exnr{2}%
\hypertarget{hvo33612}{}%
\vernacular{à hã́ã́ŋ ŋmā dɪ̄, kȅȅŋ?}%
\hypertarget{hvo33612}{}%
\modvernacular{à hã́ã́ŋ ŋmā dɪ̄, kȅȅŋ?}%
\hypertarget{hvo6447}{}%
\trs{The woman said: ``Is that so?".}%
\exnr{3}%
\hypertarget{hvo17491}{}%
\vernacular{ɲínẽ́ã́ ɪ̀ɪ̀ kàà fííléŋ kéŋ̀?}%
\hypertarget{hvo17491}{}%
\modvernacular{ɲí\-nẽ́ã́ ɪ̀ɪ̀ kàà fíí\-léŋ kéŋ̀?}%
\hypertarget{hvo803}{}%
\trs{Why do you peek at me like that?}%
\exnr{4}%
\hypertarget{hvo13945}{}%
\vernacular{gbèlìnsé átōrò máŋá kéŋ̀.}%
\hypertarget{hvo13945}{}%
\modvernacular{gbè\-lìn\-sé á\-tōrò má\-ŋá kéŋ̀.}%
\hypertarget{hvo11768}{}%
\trs{It is three o'clock.}%

\pos{cpx.v}%
\literalmeaning{take drop}%
%
%
\sensenr{1}%
\hypertarget{hvo35809}{}%
\definition{to stop}%
\lsgloss{stop}%
{\startexample}%
\hypertarget{hvo17034}{}%
\vernacular{kpá ɪ̀ɪ̀ sɪ̀ŋɲʊ̃̀hã́ háŋ̀ tā.}%
\hypertarget{hvo17034}{}%
\modvernacular{kpá ɪ̀ɪ̀ sɪ̀ŋɲʊ̃̀hã́ háŋ̀ tā.}%
\hypertarget{hvo19767}{}%
\trs{Stop this drinking habit of yours.}%
\sensenr{2}%
\hypertarget{hvo5053}{}%
\definition{to drop}%
\lsgloss{drop}%
{\startexample}%
\hypertarget{hvo2452}{}%
\vernacular{kpa a bɪɪ ta.}%
\hypertarget{hvo2452}{}%
\modvernacular{kpa a bɪɪ ta.}%
\hypertarget{hvo20208}{}%
\trs{Drop the stone.}%

\trs{The plastic bucket is not strong.}%
\exnr{2}%
\hypertarget{hvo24854}{}%
\vernacular{à hááŋ wà kpégé à ɲúú nì ʊ̀ wà kʊ́ɔ́rɪ́ sɪ̀ɪ̀máà.}%
\hypertarget{hvo24854}{}%
\modvernacular{à hááŋ wà kpé\-gé à ɲúú nì ʊ̀ wà kʊ́ɔ́\-rɪ́ sɪ̀ɪ̀máà.}%
\hypertarget{hvo19328}{}%
\trs{The woman has her menses therefore she is not cooking.}%
\typeant{\hyperlink{hvo13663}{jɔgɔsɪ\textsuperscript{1}}}%
\sensenr{2}%
\hypertarget{hvo35696}{}%
\definition{to overcome, to cure, to be able}%
\lsgloss{overcome; cure; able}%
{\startexample}%
\hypertarget{hvo42812}{}%
\vernacular{dɪ̀ ʊ̀ wá kpēgē ʊ̀ kàá kààlɪ̀ kùmásí ré.}%
\hypertarget{hvo42812}{}%
\modvernacular{dɪ̀ ʊ̀ wá kpē\-gē ʊ̀ kàá kàà\-lɪ̀ kù\-másí ré.}%
\hypertarget{hvo31946}{}%
\trs{If he recovers, he will go to Kumasi.}%

\ipa{kpɪ́sɪ́}%
%
%
\synpos{v}%
\hypertarget{hvo37816}{}%
\definition{to sneeze}%
\lsgloss{sneeze}%
{\startexample}%
\hypertarget{hvo12571}{}%
\vernacular{tɪ́ɛ́ŋ tɔ̀wà ń̩ dʊ́ m̩̀m̩̀ mɪ̀bʊ̀àsá nɪ́ à kpɪ́sɪ́.}%
\hypertarget{hvo12571}{}%
\modvernacular{tɪ́ɛ́ŋ tɔ̀wà ń̩ dʊ́ m̩̀m̩̀ mɪ̀bʊ̀à\-sá nɪ́ à kpɪ́\-sɪ́.}%
\hypertarget{hvo20411}{}%
\trs{Give me tobacco to put in my nostrils to sneeze.}%

\ipa{kpʊ́}%

%

\hypertarget{hvo3866}{}%

\exnr{1}%
\hypertarget{hvo31519}{}%
\vernacular{nàŋkpááŋ ká kpʊ̄ nànsá à wà tèlè.}%
\hypertarget{hvo31519}{}%
\modvernacular{nàŋ\-kpááŋ ká kpʊ̄ nàn\-sá à wà tè\-lè.}%
\hypertarget{hvo20909}{}%
\trs{A hunter went and killed meat and came back.}%
\exnr{2}%
\hypertarget{hvo3779}{}%
\vernacular{à nɪ̀báálá bàlɪ̀ɛ̀ kpʊ́ dɔ̄ŋā rà.}%
\hypertarget{hvo3779}{}%
\modvernacular{à nɪ̀báá\-lá bà\-lɪ̀ɛ̀ kpʊ́ dɔ̄\-ŋā rà.}%
\hypertarget{hvo7108}{}%
\trs{The two men killed each other.}%
\sensenr{2}%
\hypertarget{hvo18076}{}%
\definition{to overtake or overwhelm, as with perceptual stimuli, to affect strongly}%
\lsgloss{overtake}%
{\startexample}%
\hypertarget{hvo7385}{}%
\vernacular{jɪ̀ɪ̀sá kpʊ́jɛ̀ʊ̄.}%
\hypertarget{hvo7385}{}%
\modvernacular{jɪ̀ɪ̀sá kpʊ́\-jɛ̀ʊ̄.}%
\hypertarget{hvo3599}{}%
\trs{It is too salty.}%
\sensenr{3}%
\hypertarget{hvo25975}{}%
\definition{to cut yam from its plant and leave the tuber in the ground for the second harvest}%
\lsgloss{cut}%
{\startexample}%
\hypertarget{hvo18228}{}%
\vernacular{kpʊ́ kpááŋ dʊ̄.}%
\hypertarget{hvo18228}{}%
\modvernacular{kpʊ́ kpááŋ dʊ̄.}%
\hypertarget{hvo15903}{}%
\trs{Cut the yam and leave it in the yam mound.}%

\begin{letter}{l}
\newentry
\headword{la}%
%
\varofblockopener{}%
 \typevarof{\hyperlink{hvo12796}{ra}}%
\varofblockcloser{}%
%------------------------------
\newentry
\hypertarget{hvo24969}{}%
\headword{laa}%
\hypertarget{hvo8947}{}%
\ipa{làà}%
\pos{v}%
%
%
\sensenr{1}%
\hypertarget{hvo11242}{}%
\definition{to take something from a source, to receive}%
\lsgloss{collect; take; receive}%
{\startexample}%
\hypertarget{hvo88}{}%
\vernacular{làà ɪ̀ɪ̀ mòlìbíí tótíí.}%
\hypertarget{hvo88}{}%
\modvernacular{làà ɪ̀ɪ̀ mò\-lìbíí tó\-tíí.}%
\hypertarget{hvo23130}{}%
\trs{Take your share of money.}%
\sensenr{2}%
\hypertarget{hvo39855}{}%
\definition{to take a road or a direction}%
\lsgloss{take a direction}%
{\startexample}
\exnr{1}%
\hypertarget{hvo32799}{}%
\vernacular{kùlkpóŋ tìwíí ǹ̩ làà kààlɪ̀ wàá.}%
\hypertarget{hvo32799}{}%
\modvernacular{kùl\-kpóŋ tì\-wíí ǹ̩ làà kàà\-lɪ̀ wàá.}%
\hypertarget{hvo27715}{}%
\trs{I took the Kulkpong road to go to Wa.}%
\exnr{2}%
\hypertarget{hvo39701}{}%
\vernacular{ń̩ láá kùó ká wàà.}%
\hypertarget{hvo39701}{}%
\modvernacular{ń̩ láá kùó ká wàà.}%
\hypertarget{hvo13827}{}%
\trs{I am going to the farm and will come back.}%
\sensenr{3}%
\hypertarget{hvo10719}{}%
\definition{to answer, to respond to, to reply}%
\lsgloss{reply; answer; respond to}%
{\startexample}%
\hypertarget{hvo3531}{}%
\vernacular{ǹ̩ kàá làà ɪ̀ɪ̀ jɪ́rɪ́ɪ́ rā.}%
\hypertarget{hvo3531}{}%
\modvernacular{ǹ̩ kàá làà ɪ̀ɪ̀ jɪ́\-rɪ́ɪ́ rā.}%
\hypertarget{hvo43052}{}%
\trs{I will attend to your call.}%
\sensenr{4}%
\hypertarget{hvo20212}{}%
\definition{to agree with (collocate with \textsl{nʊ̃ã})}%
\lsgloss{agree with}%
{\startexample}%
\hypertarget{hvo15815}{}%
\vernacular{bà làà nʊ̃̀ã̀ nɪ̄.}%
\hypertarget{hvo15815}{}%
\modvernacular{bà làà nʊ̃̀ã̀ nɪ̄.}%
\hypertarget{hvo5071}{}%
\trs{They agreed.}%
\sensenr{5}%
\hypertarget{hvo23084}{}%
\definition{to yield well (for plants)}%
\lsgloss{yield}%
{\startexample}%
\hypertarget{hvo4853}{}%
\vernacular{ʊ̀ʊ̀ mɪ̃́ã́ lááwɔ́ʊ́.}%
\hypertarget{hvo4853}{}%
\modvernacular{ʊ̀ʊ̀ mɪ̃́ã́ láá\-wɔ́ʊ́.}%

\ipa{láŋgbɛ̀}%
\pos{n}%
%
%
\sensenr{1}%
\hypertarget{hvo14413}{}%
\definition{Rufous Scrub Robin}%
\lsgloss{bird (type of)}%
\sciname{Cercotrichas galactotes}%
{\definitioncloser}
\sensenr{2}%
\hypertarget{hvo4135}{}%
\definition{good singer}%
\lsgloss{singer (good)}%
{\definitioncloser}
\plural{\textsl{laŋ\-gbɛsa; laŋ\-gbɛsa}}%
%------------------------------
\newentry
\homograph{1}%
\headword{laŋsɪ}%
\hypertarget{hvo28300}{}%
\ipa{làŋsɪ̀}%
%
%
\sensenr{1}%
\synpos{pl.v}%
\hypertarget{hvo24205}{}%
\definition{to gather bit by bit, to collect from place to place}%
\lsgloss{gather}%
{\startexample}
\exnr{1}%
\hypertarget{hvo9620}{}%
\vernacular{à nárá káá lāŋsùū.}%
\hypertarget{hvo9620}{}%
\modvernacular{à ná\-rá káá lāŋ\-sùū.}%
\hypertarget{hvo7455}{}%
\trs{The people are gathering.}%
\exnr{2}%
\hypertarget{hvo33770}{}%
\vernacular{làŋsè à tɔ́ʊ̀ nɪ́hɪ̃̀ɛ̃̀sā, bá wá làgàmɪ̀.}%
\hypertarget{hvo33770}{}%
\modvernacular{làŋ\-sè à tɔ́ʊ̀ nɪ́\-hɪ̃̀ɛ̃̀sā, bá wá là\-gàmɪ̀.}%
\hypertarget{hvo18019}{}%
\trs{Gather the village elders, they have to meet.}%
\sensenr{2}%
\synpos{v}%
\hypertarget{hvo21622}{}%
\definition{to scatter}%
\lsgloss{scatter}%
{\startexample}%
\hypertarget{hvo9141}{}%
\vernacular{làŋsè à díŋ tā.}%
\hypertarget{hvo9141}{}%
\modvernacular{làŋ\-sè à díŋ tā.}%
\hypertarget{hvo7165}{}%
\trs{Put out the fire.}%

\ipa{lúdí}%
%
%
\synpos{v}%
\hypertarget{hvo29615}{}%
\definition{to make a hole in something}%
\lsgloss{make hole}%
{\startexample}%
\hypertarget{hvo44664}{}%
\vernacular{lúdí à kùbé.}%
\hypertarget{hvo44664}{}%
\modvernacular{lú\-dí à kù\-bé.}%
\hypertarget{hvo37249}{}%
\trs{Make a hole in the coconut.}%
%------------------------------
\newentry
\homograph{1}%
\headword{lugo}%
\hypertarget{hvo19579}{}%
\ipa{lùgò}%
\pos{v}%
%
%
\sensenr{1}%
\hypertarget{hvo43887}{}%
\definition{to bore a hole, to hollow out}%
\lsgloss{bore}%
{\startexample}%
\hypertarget{hvo21837}{}%
\vernacular{dààsã́ã́rá lúgó dáá rá à sã̀ã̀ tìmpántíé.}%
\hypertarget{hvo21837}{}%
\modvernacular{dàà\-sã́ã́\-rá lú\-gó dáá rá à sã̀ã̀ tìm\-pán\-tíé.}%
\hypertarget{hvo28839}{}%
\trs{The carvers hollowed out a tree and carved talking drums.}%
\sensenr{2}%
\hypertarget{hvo38713}{}%
\definition{to change one's name}%
\lsgloss{change name}%
{\startexample}%
\hypertarget{hvo33303}{}%
\vernacular{ùù lúgó ʊ̀ʊ̀ sɔ́n ná.}%
\hypertarget{hvo33303}{}%
\modvernacular{ùù lú\-gó ʊ̀ʊ̀ sɔ́n ná.}%
\hypertarget{hvo962}{}%
\trs{He changed his name.}%
\sensenr{3}%
\hypertarget{hvo1232}{}%
\definition{to withdraw one's words}%
\lsgloss{withdraw}%
{\startexample}%
\hypertarget{hvo10069}{}%
\vernacular{ǹ̩ lúgó ǹǹ nʊ̃̀ã̀ rā.}%
\hypertarget{hvo10069}{}%
\modvernacular{ǹ̩ lú\-gó ǹǹ nʊ̃̀ã̀ rā.}%
\hypertarget{hvo12878}{}%
\trs{I withdrawn my words.}%

\ipa{lʊ̀gà}%

%
%
\sensenr{1}%
\hypertarget{hvo27775}{}%
\definition{to forge and shape iron}%
\lsgloss{forge}%
{\startexample}%
\hypertarget{hvo10500}{}%
\vernacular{lʊ́lʊ́tá káá lʊ̄gà prɛ́gà.}%
\hypertarget{hvo10500}{}%
\modvernacular{lʊ́\-lʊ́\-tá káá lʊ̄\-gà prɛ́\-gà.}%
\hypertarget{hvo21891}{}%
\trs{A blacksmith is forging finger bells.}%
\sensenr{2}%
\hypertarget{hvo5650}{}%
\definition{to struggle or strive, to be engaged with a problem or a task}%
\lsgloss{struggle; strive}%
{\startexample}%
\hypertarget{hvo28395}{}%
\vernacular{lʊ̀gà já pétí jà tʊ́má làgá nɪ̀.}%
\hypertarget{hvo28395}{}%
\modvernacular{lʊ̀gà já pé\-tí jà tʊ́\-má là\-gá nɪ̀.}%
\hypertarget{hvo32082}{}%
\trs{Strive, so we can finish our work fast.}%
\sensenr{3}%
\hypertarget{hvo20910}{}%
\definition{to wrestle}%
\lsgloss{wrestle}%
{\startexample}%
\hypertarget{hvo44499}{}%
\vernacular{hàmɔ̃́wísè jáà lʊ́gà dèndíl ní rē.}%
\hypertarget{hvo44499}{}%
\modvernacular{hà\-mɔ̃́\-wísè jáà lʊ́\-gà dèn\-díl ní rē.}%
\hypertarget{hvo27654}{}%
\trs{Children usually wrestle outside.}%
